    & & & \multicolumn{2}{p{0.3\linewidth}}{\cellcolor[rgb]{0.95,0.95,0.95}{%

	  \tt {\tiny [GM$|$GM]}  
	 Model produced DONE action at turn 49, end episode. 
	  } 
	   } 
	   }
